- [Eye Health](https://v5irgb-4a.myshopify.com/products/eye-health): Nutra Moment eye health capsules provide a variety of benefits that complement proper ocular care.† Its wide range of effects is the consequence of the carefully chosen chemicals that comprise its recipe. These supplements are extremely helpful in letting you know that even if you've been eating a healthy diet, the nutrients you're getting will be beneficial to your eye health.† In today's digital era, many people are experiencing eye fatigue and dry eyes from overexposure to blue light and screen use; in addition to Lutein and Zeaxanthin, we have incorporated Zinc, Copper, and Vitamin A, Vitamin E, and more, all packed into compact capsules.† After all, the eye is a highly sensitive organ that serves as your primary source of vision. Therefore, protecting the health of those organs should be one of your top priorities in life.† Support Macular Health † This unique blend combines eye-friendly vitamins and minerals to nourish your eyes, including Lutein and Zeaxanthin. These powerful carotenoid antioxidants concentrate in the macula, the area of the retina with the sharpest vision, and help the eye filter out blue light wavelengths. Promote Healthy Vision † Lutein has been shown to help promote eye and vision health.†Lutein aids in the production of the retina pigment, which acts as a filter by absorbing harmful UV rays. Everyone is born with a certain amount of Lutein in their eyes, but the body does not produce it, so you must get it from food or supplements. If you do not consume enough lutein-rich foods, the amount in your eyes may decrease as you age.† Essential Ingridients Vitamin A vitamin A is generally known for boosting eye health and may also contribute to preventing cataracts and macular degeneration.† Vitamin C vitamin C is a strong antioxidant. Antioxidants are crucial to the body's defences against free radicals, which can damage the body – including the eyes – at a cellular level.† Vitamin E Studies have demonstrated that it plays a function in safeguarding the eye against macular degeneration, the development of cataracts, and other age-associated eye illnesses while promoting overall eye health.† Selenium Has an impact comparable to that of Zinc in that it is necessary to absorb another nutrient. This example is vitamin E, the third element in this composition.† Lutein and Zeaxanthin Lutein and Zeaxanthin are two forms of carotenoids that have become well-known for their individual and combined eye health support. The ordinary American diet does not include enough of these carotenoids to provide the optimum benefit to the eye. They are believed to function to inhibit light-induced oxidative damage that is regarded to be among the fundamental causes of macular degeneration.† As we get older, the body gradually loses the store of Lutein. While Lutein can be found in various fruits, vegetables, and other sources, including marigolds, taking a daily supplement may support the retention of Lutein.† How To Use As per dietary supplement, take two (2) veggie capsules once a day. For best results, take 20-30 minutes before a meal or as directed by your health care professional.

- [Embrace Change Mental Health Awareness Sticker](https://v5irgb-4a.myshopify.com/products/embrace-change-mental-health-awareness-sticker): GENERAL PURPOSE STICKERSOur stickers are designed to stick to almost any flat, clean surface, including walls, mirrors, windows, doors, cars, bikes, and more. Whether you're looking to add a personal touch to your home, office, or vehicle, our decals offer a simple and stylish way to do so. AVAILABLE SIZESOur decals come in the following sizes: 150mm – Ideal for small accent pieces or delicate designs. 190mm – A great mid-size option for larger spaces or bolder designs. 280mm – Perfect for making a statement or using as a focal point. 85mm (Pack of 2) – Compact and convenient for smaller applications or groupings. 100mm (Pack of 2) – A bit larger than the 85mm pack, great for adding accents in multiple locations. COLOUR OPTIONS & CUSTOMISATIONWith no less than 27 colour options to choose from, our decals are fully customisable to match your style and needs. We also offer custom sizes and designs upon request, so you can create the perfect decal for any project. CHOOSE FRONT-FACING OR REVERSEDOur decals are available in both front-facing and reversed orientations (for interior window application). Simply leave a note with your order specifying your preference, and we’ll take care of the rest! DURABILITY & MATERIALEach decal is made with 100% waterproof, 3-5 year exterior-grade self-adhesive vinyl, making them suitable for both interior and exterior use. SIZING INFORMATIONThe sizes denote the maximum width or height of the sticker and represent the longest side. For example, a 280mm sticker will measure at least 280mm on its longest side, with the shorter side proportionally adjusted to avoid distorting the original design. HOW TO APPLY STICKERS?These decals can be applied to virtually any clean, flat surface. Simply peel and stick to apply – no mess, no fuss!

- [Things Will Get Better Mental Health Awareness Sticker](https://v5irgb-4a.myshopify.com/products/things-will-get-better-mental-health-awareness-sticker): GENERAL PURPOSE STICKERSOur stickers are designed to stick to almost any flat, clean surface, including walls, mirrors, windows, doors, cars, bikes, and more. Whether you're looking to add a personal touch to your home, office, or vehicle, our decals offer a simple and stylish way to do so. AVAILABLE SIZESOur decals come in the following sizes: 150mm – Ideal for small accent pieces or delicate designs. 190mm – A great mid-size option for larger spaces or bolder designs. 280mm – Perfect for making a statement or using as a focal point. 85mm (Pack of 2) – Compact and convenient for smaller applications or groupings. 100mm (Pack of 2) – A bit larger than the 85mm pack, great for adding accents in multiple locations. COLOUR OPTIONS & CUSTOMISATIONWith no less than 27 colour options to choose from, our decals are fully customisable to match your style and needs. We also offer custom sizes and designs upon request, so you can create the perfect decal for any project. CHOOSE FRONT-FACING OR REVERSEDOur decals are available in both front-facing and reversed orientations (for interior window application). Simply leave a note with your order specifying your preference, and we’ll take care of the rest! DURABILITY & MATERIALEach decal is made with 100% waterproof, 3-5 year exterior-grade self-adhesive vinyl, making them suitable for both interior and exterior use. SIZING INFORMATIONThe sizes denote the maximum width or height of the sticker and represent the longest side. For example, a 280mm sticker will measure at least 280mm on its longest side, with the shorter side proportionally adjusted to avoid distorting the original design. HOW TO APPLY STICKERS?These decals can be applied to virtually any clean, flat surface. Simply peel and stick to apply – no mess, no fuss!

Ashwagandha, also known as Withania somnifera, is a powerful herb that has been used for centuries in Ayurvedic medicine. Renowned for its ability to help the body manage stress, this adaptogenic herb can greatly enhance your overall well-being. But Ashwagandha offers more than just stress relief; it also promotes a balanced mood, boosts cognitive function, and supports immune health. Ashwagandha contains a group of chemicals called withanolides, which have been shown to reduce inflammation and fight infection. These compounds work in harmony with the body to enhance its natural defenses, making it an excellent choice for anyone looking to support their immune system. Furthermore, studies indicate that Ashwagandha can lower cortisol levels, the stress hormone, thereby reducing anxiety and improving mood. In addition to its stress-reducing properties, Ashwagandha has been found to improve sleep quality. For those battling insomnia or other sleep disorders, this herb offers a natural alternative to pharmaceutical solutions. Improved sleep can lead to better mental clarity, enhanced memory, and even a more robust immune system. Ashwagandha can also have a positive impact on physical performance. Athletes and fitness enthusiasts often turn to this herb for its ability to increase strength and endurance. Research suggests that regular intake can improve muscle recovery and reduce exercise-induced muscle damage, allowing individuals to train harder and recover faster. Moreover, the antioxidant properties of Ashwagandha help to protect the body against oxidative stress, which is responsible for many age-related diseases. By neutralizing free radicals, the herb can contribute to longevity and a healthier aging process. Integrating Ashwagandha into your daily routine couldn't be easier. Whether you prefer it in capsule form, as a powder mixed into smoothies, or as a tea, its versatility makes it simple to incorporate into your lifestyle. While it is widely considered safe, it's always a good idea to consult a healthcare provider before starting any new supplement, particularly if you are pregnant, nursing, or taking other medications. In conclusion, Ashwagandha offers a plethora of benefits that can enhance both your mental and physical health. From reducing stress and anxiety, improving sleep and cognitive function, to boosting immune health and physical performance, this ancient herb proves to be a powerhouse in natural wellness. Start your journey with Ashwagandha today and experience the remarkable difference it can make in your life.

Known for their unmatched comfort and flexibility, yoga leggings are specially designed to support you in every move, whether you're striking a pose on the mat or simply running errands. One of the standout features of yoga leggings is their ability to stretch and conform to your body, providing a snug fit without compromising on freedom of movement. The fabric is often a mix of spandex and polyester, ensuring that the leggings retain their elasticity and shape even after numerous washes. This means you can bend, twist, and stretch without any restrictions, allowing you to focus solely on your practice or exercise routine. Comfort is at the core of yoga leggings' design. The waistband is usually high-rise and supportive, which helps keep the leggings in place during intense workouts. This feature also provides a flattering figure, giving you confidence whether you're in the gym or on the go. Additionally, many yoga leggings come with moisture-wicking properties, keeping you dry and comfortable no matter how tough the session gets. Yoga leggings aren't just functional; they're also stylish. Available in a wide range of colors, patterns, and designs, you can easily find a pair that reflects your personality and style. Whether you prefer a classic black pair for a sleek look or a bold pattern to make a statement, there are yoga leggings out there for everyone. The seamless construction often found in these leggings minimizes chafing and adds to the sleek appearance, allowing you to transition effortlessly from workout to casual wear. Another benefit of yoga leggings is their versatility. They are not limited to yoga sessions alone. Due to their comfort and aesthetic appeal, many individuals wear them for various activities, including running, walking, or even lounging at home. They are incredibly easy to pair with different tops and jackets, making them an essential piece in any wardrobe. Durability is another high point of yoga leggings. Quality yoga leggings are built to withstand rigorous use and frequent washing without losing their fit or color. This makes them a worthwhile investment for anyone who values performance and longevity in their activewear. In conclusion, yoga leggings provide a blend of comfort, flexibility, and style that can enhance your performance and confidence in any setting. Whether you're a seasoned yogi or just starting out, finding the right pair of yoga leggings can make a significant difference in your overall experience. So, why wait? Dive into the world of yoga leggings and discover how they can elevate your active lifestyle.

These leggings offer unmatched comfort and style, making them perfect for yoga sessions, gym workouts, or casual wear. Crafted from high-quality materials, yoga leggings provide the right amount of stretch and support, so you can move with ease and confidence. When it comes to selecting the best yoga leggings, there are several factors to consider. First, the fabric should be breathable and moisture-wicking, ensuring you stay cool, dry, and comfortable during your workouts. Whether you're striking a pose or hitting the treadmill, the right leggings will keep you performing at your best. Another important aspect is the fit and design. Yoga leggings come in various lengths and styles, from full-length leggings to capris and shorts. Choose the design that best suits your activity and personal style. Look for features such as high waistbands, which provide additional support and a flattering shape, or pockets for convenience. Eco-conscious consumers will be pleased to know that many yoga leggings are now made from sustainable materials. Brands are increasingly focusing on reducing their environmental impact, offering leggings made from recycled fabrics or organic cotton. This allows you to feel good about your purchase, knowing that it is more sustainable. The durability of yoga leggings cannot be overstated. Quality is key, and investing in a pair that resists pilling, fading, and stretching will ensure they last longer. Check customer reviews and ratings to find leggings that maintain their shape and color after multiple washes and wears. In addition to workouts, yoga leggings are perfect for everyday wear. Pair them with a casual top or jacket for a comfortable, stylish outfit that can take you from the yoga studio to brunch with friends. The versatility of yoga leggings makes them a favorite in any wardrobe. Many brands offer yoga leggings in a vast range of colors and prints, so you can express your individuality and style. Whether you prefer classic black or vibrant patterns, there are options to suit every taste. In conclusion, investing in a good pair of yoga leggings is essential for anyone who values comfort, style, and performance. They are not only a staple for yoga enthusiasts but also a versatile piece of activewear that can transition seamlessly into everyday outfits. Prioritize quality and sustainability, and you’ll find the perfect leggings to suit your needs.
